  -update mesa to 21.1.0-rc3

   (and reload when it exceeds treshold). Feature is condigured by
   MM_MYTHTV_STANDBY_ACTION variable. If set to 'rss_reload' then
   when mythfrontend enters standby, mm2 checks RSS and if RSS exceeds
   MM_MYTHTV_RSS_FOR_RESTART - mm2 reloads mythfronted to release RSS.
  -update libdrm to 2.4.110
  -update iwd to 1.27

  -add support for openvfd. If MM_LCDPROC_ENABLED variable is set to 'openvfd'
   MiniMyth2 will use openvfd to control simple LED displays.
   Configuration of openvfd is takend for device-tree unless
   MM_LCDPROC_FETCH_LCDD_CONF vaiable is set. If it is set, then MiniMyth2
   will download openvfd.conf from conf-ro dir and will use this file as
   configuration for openvfd.

11.22.2(20211017)
Minimyth2-master:
  -update mythtv to r2898
Minimyth2-*:
  -switch gstreamer build system to Meson (except gst-libav)
  -update all gstreamer components to 1.19.2 (except gst-libav)
  -update mesa to 21.2.3
  -update qt6 to 6.2
  -make mythtv-test working nicelly on qt6.2
  -update 5.14 kernel to 5.14.10
  -add 5sec delay before intering sleep. IRblaster commands are sent
   asynchroneously to mm_sleep execution - so if IR balster command sequence
   takes longer execution that mm_sleep reaches s2ram - mm2 enters sleep
   in the middle of IR commad execution. This hack adds 5sec sleep to get
   IRblaster working at suspend2ram with crude assumption that OFF command
   sequence executed by IR blaster takes less that 5sec...
  -update mesa-git to 21.3.0-rc1
  -update busybox to 1.34.1
  -remove disablement of AFBC on H616 devices
  -update makemkv-bin to 1.16.4
  -update makemkv-oss to 1.16.4

11.22.1(20210928)
Minimyth2-master:
  -update mythtv to r2891
Minimyth2-*:
  -update 5.14 kernel to 5.14.7
  -switch mm2 from using 7y old mysql to mariadb
  -add mariadb 10.6.4
  -add qt6 6.1.3
  -add liblz4 1.9.3 required by latest versions of mysql
  -add libedit 20210910-3.1 required by latest versions of mysql
  -add zstd 1.5.0 required by latest versions of mysql
  -add boost 1.73.0 required by latest versions of mysql
  -add double-conversion required by Qt6
  -add pcre2 required by Qt6
  -switch MythTV cache prunning metodology
    By default mm2 uses RAMDISK for mythtv home dir with 256MB size. This small size
    causes RAMDISK becomes quite quickly full and this breaks some MythTV functionalites.
    Build-in mythtv cache prunning is based on age of files and cache prunning is triggered
    only at Mythv start. As mm2 uses sleep/resume - cache prunning efectively is not working.
    This commit add very simple daemon which periodically scans MythTV cache, looks on it's total
    occupation - and if treshold (default 128MB) is exceeded - deletes one-by-one largest files
    till occupation becomes below tresholed. Treshold can be changed by MM_MYTHTV_CACHE_FOR_PRUNE
    find: switch to use find from findutils as busybox hasn't -printf functionality
  -add support fot multiple Qt versions. It is selectable by mm_QT_VERSION variable in 
    minimyth.conf.mk
  -update mesa to 21.2.2
  -reduce image size by not copying python tests
  -reduce image size by copying only relevant to supported boards brcm firmwares
  -add perl-common-sense: add as it is required by perl-Strip
  -add perl-Strip: add as it is required by perl-Strip
  -add perl-Params-Util: add as it is required by perl-Strip
  -add perl-PPI: add as it is required by perl-Strip
  -add perl-IO-String: add as it is required by perl-Strip
  -add perl-Clone: add as it is required by perl-Strip
  -switch from perl-tidy to perl-Strip. This improves considerably stripping efficiency:
    perl-tidy: 68M->60M
    perl-Strip: 68M->50M
  -add symlinking all mesa/dri and vdpau drivers to single all-in-one drivers
    Mesa generates dri/vdpau drivers as single binaries serving all supported GPUs.
    This commit replaces in image all dri drivers with symlink to single
    universal dri driver. This allows to reduce xz packed image size from
    235M to 196M.
  -fix frequent crasches in QtWebKit
  -update QtWebKit to g5a4cfb588

11.21.0(20210829)

  -update mythtv to r2839
Minimyth2-*:
  -add MM_MYTHTV_CACHE_FOR_PRUNE variable for trigering periodic cache pruning.
    If set and when MiniMyth2 enters suspend-to-ram, MiniMyth2 will check size of
    MythTV frontend cache. If total size of this directory & subdirectories
    is exceeding MM_MYTHTV_CACHE_FOR_PRUNE, suspend-to-ram script will ask MythTV frontend to reload theme
    for prune cache dir. Default value is '128'
  -update image makefile: make RAM/TFTP/NFS distribution not dependent on SHARE distribution
  -image: don't include dm140.so in lcdproc files

  -switch from wm from ratpoison to blackbox

   updates for SD card & USB key booted systems usind rsync.
   Content for online updates is prepared by MiniMyth2 GAR build system
   if '<strong>mm_INSTALL_ONLINE_UPDATES</strong>' is set to 'yes'.
   Location of online update files is defined by '<strong>mm_ONLINE_UPDATES</strong>' variable.
   On-line update files should be avaliable at root location of module 'mm2-updates'
   of rsync daemon running in chroot mode on remote server.

9.0.0(20180625)
Minimyth2-master:
  This version has support for minimyth2 compilation for armv7 and aarch64 targets.
  Basically - to get mm2 compiled for i.e aarch64 target - You need set mm_GARCH=armv8
  and do full recompile.
  To test creation of full cross-build chain and all packages recompilation for given
  target architecture, I tested aarch64 build of mm2 on bcm2837 (rpi3) with u-boot
  from ArchLinux ARM and got fully working mm2 with stock 4.16 kernel of course except
  video playback (this is well know issue. see: https://github.com/raspberrypi/firmware/issues/550).
  -update kernel to 4.16.3
  -add 4.16 kernel configs for armv7/aarch64 platforms
  -fix multiple packages to compile for aarch64 target
  -add to build system support for building armv7 and aarch64 targets
  -update gstreamer to 1.10.2
  -update gst-libav to 1.10.2
  -update gst-plugins-base to 1.10.2
  -update gst-plugins-good to 1.10.2
  -update gst-plugins-bad to 1.10.2
  -update ImageMagick to 6.9.10-2
  -update libffi to 3.2.1
  -update libpng to 1.0.22
  -update portaudio to v190600_20161030
  -update libtirpc to 1.0.3
  -update nfs-utils to 2.3.2
  -update rpcbind to 0.2.4
  -remove nvidia-340.106 and nvidia-390.48
  -add nvidia-340.107
  -add nvidia-396.24
  -update PerlMagick to 6.89
  -update curl to 7.60
  -update python2 to 2.7.15. Finally!
  -add python 3.6.5 but stay with python2 as defaut
  -update python-cffi to 1.11.5
  -update mc to 4.8.21
  -update rsync to 3.1.3
  -update usbutils to 009
  -update v4l-utils to 1.6.3
  -add xorgproto 2018.4
  -switch all Xorg packages to xorgproto
  -update font-util to 1.3.1
  -update iceauth to 1.0.8
  -update mkfontdir to 1.1.3
  -udpate xbitmaps to 1.1.2
  -udpate xkbcomp to 1.4.1

8.11.0(20170808)
Minimyth2-master:
  -update mythtv to r12
Minimyth2-29:
  -update mythtv to r15
  -add myth-29-fixes to build system
Minimyth2-0.28-fixes:
  -update mythtv to r160
Minimyth2-*:
  -update kernel to 4.12.5
  -update mesa to 17.1.6
  -fix lirc auto-repeat in devinput mode
  -change strategy VideoPlaybackProfile setting at first mm2 run. Now - if
   MM_VIDEO_PLAYBACK_PROFILE is empty (or set to 'userdefined') - at first run
   mm2 will set VideoPlaybackProfile to build-in profile matching detected HW.
   At next runs will not touch VideoPlaybackProfile anymore. 
   First mm2 run detection is based on checking JUMP MAINMENU jumppoint.
   If it is set to 'Alt+H' (mm2 defaults this jumppoint to Alt+H by mm2 lirc
   subsystem) - mm2 assumes it is NOT first run.
   If MM_VIDEO_PLAYBACK_PROFILE='auto' - then mm2 will always switch
   VideoPlaybackProfile to predefined mythtv profiles acordingly to detected video HW.
   If MM_VIDEO_PLAYBACK_PROFILE='profile' - then mm2 will always switch
   VideoPlaybackProfile to predefined mythtv profiles acordingly to 'profile'.
  -removing auto-generation of MiniMyth VideoPlaybackProfile. It brings no value today while
   requires patching of mythtv sources and makes boot process longer.
  -remove MM_VIDEO_DECODER and MM_VIDEO_DEINTERLACER variables as they are no more used/valid.
  -added following non-obovious key lircrc mappings:
     KEY_RED = D (delete)
     KEY_GREEN = I (info)
     KEY_YELLOW = T (subtitles)
     KEY_BLUE = A (time stretch)

8.10.0(20170701)
Minimyth2-master:
  -update mythtv to r511
Minimyth2-0.28-fixes:
  -update mythtv to r155
Minimyth2-master, Minimyth2-0.28-fixes:
  -update eventlircd to current master
  -add configs/udev rules needed by eventlircd
  -move lirc subsystem to eventlircd. Now mm2 supportsw full hot-plug of
   mulitple IR remotes/HID acting IR/etc.
  -syncing build-in lircd.conf keys to current kernel input.h. Now 
   mm2 should work plug-and-play out-of-box on any remote supported by kernel.
  -syncing lircrc to devinput namespace. Now mm2 should out-of-box
   understand keys from any remote supported by kernel.
  -switch lirc subsystem default to eventlirc. Now mm2 is fully out-of-box
   plug-and-play and hot-plug for thousesnd of IR cremotes supported by kernel.
  -added MM_LIRC_USE_DEVINPUT variable allowing to switch to classical
  (LIRCD daemon based mode). Such switch is required for setups with irblaster
   as devinput not supports irsending. MM_LIRC_USE_DEVINPUT is default ="yes" until
   any irblaster command is defined/enabled. When such irblaster command is
   defined/enabled - MM_LIRC_USE_DEVINPUT becomes "no", lirc subsystem switches to classical
   daemon mode and mm2 starts to work as previosly (using build in remote definitions, etc).
  -added mythnotify for hot-pluged devices.
  -update documentation for above lirc changes.
  -update mesa to 17.1.3
  -update libdrm to 2.4.81
  -update kernel to 4.11.7
  -enabling serial_ir driver building in kernel and adding it to image
  -added KEY_CHANNELUP/KEY_CHANNELDOWN for google-chrome/mozilla-firefox PgUP/PgDown
  -add auto-setting hostname in case when DHCP server is not assigning hostname. In such case
   mm2 will auto-set hostname to 'Myth-Frontend-<6th part of MAC address>'.
   This allows to newely added mm2 frontend to boot and become have fully functional
   WITHOUT any interventions/actions on enviroment.
   This makes mm2 to be real zero-touch-provisioning appliance.
  -Change keybindings: 'TV Playback/Play', 'TV Frontend/Playback', 'Images/Play' from 'P' to 'Ctrl+P'
  -Add 'Music/ADDTRACKSANDPLAY' key binding 'Ctrl+P'
  -Map in lircrc.mythtv KEY_PLAY as 'Ctrl+P'

8.1.1 (20160330)
Minimyth2-master:
  -add xorg.conf device section processing for Intel/Nvidia/Radeon/Vmware. Now
   irrelevant to present hardware sections are commented out. This speeds-up Xserver
   start as there is no loading and unloading Xdrivers for hardware which is not present.
  -split rc.d/conf to conf_sequential and conf_parallel to speed-up boot process.
   conf_parallel runs following conf scripts sqquentially:
   P_ACPI
   P_CPU
   P_DEBUG
   P_EXTRAS
   P_GAME
   P_LCDPROC
   P_LMSENSORS
   P_MAIL
   P_MAKEMKV
   P_MEDIA
   P_PLUGIN
   P_S3_WORKRNDS
   P_SSH_SERVER
   P_VOIP
   conf_sequential runs following conf scripts sqquentially:
   S_AUDIO
   S_LIRC (with included MM_EXTERNAL)
   S_MASTER
   S_MEDIA
   S_MINIMYTH
   S_MYTHDB
   S_MYTHTV
   S_PLUGIN
   S_SECURITY
   S_THEME
   S_X (with included MM_VIDEO)
   This allows to shorten boot time on ION1 by another 6-7sec.
  -add creation of empty remotecache dir needed by mm_show_sysstat_osd.pl
   to store channel icons when myth remotecache is on ramdisk.
  -fix typo in mm_ui_locatization_perl file.
  -fix remote key KEY_ENTER binding for info_button_actions.
  -update release notes with info about 8.1.0/8.1.1 signifficant init system
   rework

   Following variables are removed:

    MM_X_OUTPUT_TV
    MM_X_TV_TYPE
    MM_X_TV_OUTPUT

    MM_VIDEO_ASPECT_RATIO
    MM_VIDEO_FONT_SCALE
    MM_VIDEO_RESIZE_ENABLED
    MM_VIDEO_FOLLOW_FRAMERATE
    MM_MEDIA_GALLERY_MOUNTPOINT
    MM_MEDIA_GALLERY_URL
    MM_MEDIA_MUSIC_MOUNTPOINT
    MM_MEDIA_MUSIC_URL
    MM_MEDIA_VIDEO_MOUNTPOINT
    MM_MEDIA_VIDEO_URL
  -add separate categories of init scriptes: sequential and parallel.
  -reorder init sequences for quicker boot. Mapping of init sevices
  is following:
  MM_INIT_START_SEQUENTIAL:
    security
    mythdb_buffer_create
    master
    audio
    video
    mythtv
    font
    x
  MM_INIT_START_PARALLEL:
    dbus
    media
    irtrans
    lirc
    lcdproc
    acpi
    time
    web
    extras
    game
    cpu
    telnet
    ssh_server
    avahi
    mythdb_buffer_delete
   This improves boot time as paralell services are starting parallel
   to mythtv/Xserver in backgroud. On ION1 this reduces boot time from
   60-65sec to 40-45sec.
  -add procps-3.2.8-ps-cgroup-suppress-root-group.patch.patch to procps for
   suppressing "Unknown HZ value..." warning

   modifications.

3.61 (20-02-2011)
-updating kernel to 2.6.37.1
-added MM_VIDEO_FOLLOW_FRAMERATE (default='yes') for configuring scenario where
 myth@home should set TV refresh rate to content framerate but not touch screen
 modes. (TV isn't resized). Effectivelly it means scaling for all modes is done by
 myth@home. It is oposite to scenario where MM_VIDEO_FOLLOW_FRAMERATE='no' and
 MM_VIDEO_RESIZE='yes' - in such scenario myth@home will change TV framerate and 
 modes.

1.40 (13-03-2010)
 -downgrading Mesa to 7.6

1.39 (13-03-2010)
 -added option for restarting mythfrontend at sleep.
  Feature is controlled by MM_RESTART_ON_SLEEP. If
  MM_RESTART_ON_SLEEP="mythfrontend", then mm will
  kill mythfrontend before sllep and restart after 
  resume. If MM_RESTART_ON_SLEEP="xorg" then then mm will
  kill Xorg before sllep and restart after 
  resume. If is empty - mm will keep mythfrontend/Xorg 
  across sleep-resume.
 -depreciate MM_RESTART_X_ON_SLEEP as now MM_RESTART_ON_SLEEP
  can control restarting Xorg on sleep-resume
